
class Specter:
    def __init__(self, code: str) -> None:
        self.code = code
        self.execute(...)
        return None
    def execute(self, code: str = ...) -> None:
        return exec(str(code))
    
class Func:
    def calculate(num: int) -> int:
        return num*2
    def define(key, value: Any) -> Any:
        globals()[key] = value
        return globals()[key]
